# <a name="dimensions-and-measurements-available-in-call-quality-dashboard"></a><span data-ttu-id="5cae3-103">Dimensioni e misure disponibili nel dashboard qualità chiamata</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cae3-103">Dimensions and measurements available in Call Quality Dashboard</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="5cae3-104">Il dashboard qualità chiamata (Call Quality Dashboard) per Microsoft teams e Skype for business online ti permette di comprendere meglio la qualità delle chiamate effettuate con questi servizi.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cae3-104">The Call Quality Dashboard (CQD) for Microsoft Teams and Skype for Business Online allows you to better understand call quality of calls made with these services.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="5cae3-105">Questo argomento fornisce informazioni dettagliate sulle dimensioni e le misure visibili tramite Call Quality dashboard.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cae3-105">This topic provides detailed information about the dimensions and measurements visible through CQD.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="5cae3-106">Per altre informazioni su Call Quality dashboard, vedere [attivazione e utilizzo di Call Quality dashboard per Microsoft teams e Skype for business online](turning-on-and-using-call-quality-dashboard.md).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cae3-106">To learn more about CQD, see [Turning on and using Call Quality Dashboard for Microsoft Teams and Skype for Business Online](turning-on-and-using-call-quality-dashboard.md).</span></span>

## <a name="first-and-second-endpoint-classification"></a><span data-ttu-id="5cae3-107">Classificazione del primo e secondo endpoint</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cae3-107">First and Second endpoint classification</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="5cae3-108">Molte delle dimensioni e delle misure in Call Quality dashboard sono contrassegnate come First o Second.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cae3-108">Many of the dimensions and measurements in CQD are labeled as first or second.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="5cae3-109">La seguente logica determina quale endpoint coinvolto nello stream o chiamata viene etichettato come primo:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cae3-109">The following logic determines which endpoint involved in the stream or call is labeled as first:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="5cae3-110">Un endpoint server (MCU AV, Mediation Server e così via) viene considerato per primo quando un server è coinvolto nel flusso o nella chiamata.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cae3-110">A Server endpoint (AV MCU, Mediation Server, and so on) is considered First when a Server is involved in the stream or call.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="5cae3-111">Un endpoint client viene considerato secondo a meno che il flusso non si trovi tra due endpoint server.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cae3-111">A Client endpoint is considered Second unless the stream is between two Server endpoints.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="5cae3-112">Se entrambi gli endpoint sono dello stesso tipo, First vs Second viene impostato in base all'ordinamento interno della categoria dell'agente utente per verificare che l'ordinamento sia coerente.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cae3-112">If both endpoints are the same type, first vs. second is set based on internal ordering of the user agent category to ensure that the ordering is consistent.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="5cae3-113">Ad esempio, qui ogni riga rappresenta una coppia di agenti utente coinvolti in un flusso:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cae3-113">For example, here each row represents a pair of User Agents involved in a stream:</span></span>

|<span data-ttu-id="5cae3-114">Categoria agente utente del chiamante</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cae3-114">User Agent Category of Caller</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="5cae3-115">Categoria agente utente del chiamato</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cae3-115">User Agent Category of Callee</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="5cae3-116">First Endpoint</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cae3-116">First Endpoint</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="5cae3-117">Second Endpoint</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cae3-117">Second Endpoint</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="5cae3-118">First Is Caller</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cae3-118">First Is Caller</span></span>
|:--- |:--- |:--- |:--- |:--- |
|<span data-ttu-id="5cae3-119">AV-MCU</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cae3-119">AV-MCU</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="5cae3-120">OC (client Skype for Business)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cae3-120">OC (Skype for Business client)</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="5cae3-121">AV-MCU</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cae3-121">AV-MCU</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="5cae3-122">OC (client Skype for Business)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cae3-122">OC (Skype for Business client)</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="5cae3-123">TRUE</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cae3-123">TRUE</span></span> |

|<span data-ttu-id="5cae3-148">OC Phone (telefono IP Skype for Business)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cae3-148">OC Phone (Skype for Business IP Phone)</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="5cae3-149">OC (client Skype for Business)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cae3-149">OC (Skype for Business client)</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="5cae3-150">OC (client Skype for Business)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cae3-150">OC (Skype for Business client)</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="5cae3-151">OC Phone (telefono IP Skype for Business)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cae3-151">OC Phone (Skype for Business IP Phone)</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="5cae3-152">FALSE</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cae3-152">FALSE</span></span> |

> [!NOTE]
> <span data-ttu-id="5cae3-p103">Questa classificazione primo-secondo è distinta da quale endpoint sia il chiamante o il chiamato. La dimensione Il primo è il chiamante può essere usata per aiutare a individuare quale endpoint è il chiamante o il chiamato.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cae3-p103">That First and Second classification is separate from which endpoint is the caller or callee. The First Is Caller dimension can be used to help identify which endpoint was the caller or callee.</span></span>

## <a name="dimensions"></a><span data-ttu-id="5cae3-155">Dimensioni</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cae3-155">Dimensions</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="5cae3-156">Le informazioni sulle dimensioni si basano in parte sui dati caricati nel portale di Call Quality dashboard.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cae3-156">Dimensions information is based in part on data uploaded to the CQD portal.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="5cae3-157">Molti valori di dimensione possono essere usati anche come filtri.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cae3-157">Many Dimension values can also be used as filters.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="5cae3-158">La tabella seguente elenca le dimensioni attualmente disponibili in Call Quality dashboard, nell'ordine indicato nell'editor di query usato per creare report o modificare i report definiti in precedenza.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cae3-158">The following table lists the dimensions currently available in CQD, in the order listed in the Query Editor used to create reports or edit previously defined reports.</span></span>

| <span data-ttu-id="5cae3-2194">OS Pair</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cae3-2194">OS Pair</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="5cae3-2195">Coppia enumerata</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cae3-2195">Enumerated pair</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="5cae3-2196">Coppia del nome e della versione del sistema operativo del primo e del secondo endpoint.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cae3-2196">Pair of the OS name and version for first and second endpoint.</span></span> <br/> <span data-ttu-id="5cae3-2197">**Valore di esempio:** Windows 10: Windows 10</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cae3-2197">**Example value:** Windows 10 : Windows 10</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="5cae3-2198">&bull;Il nome del sistema operativo non può essere analizzato o non è stato segnalato dall'endpoint</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cae3-2198">&bull; OS name could not be parsed or was not reported by endpoint</span></span>  |
| <span data-ttu-id="5cae3-2199">Tenant Id Pair</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cae3-2199">Tenant Id Pair</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="5cae3-2200">Coppia enumerata</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cae3-2200">Enumerated pair</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="5cae3-2201">Coppia di ID tenant per il primo e il secondo endpoint.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cae3-2201">Pair of the tenant ids for first and second endpoint.</span></span> <br/> <span data-ttu-id="5cae3-2202">**Valore di esempio:** 00000000 — 0000-0000-0000 — 000000000000:00000000 — 0000-0000-0000 — 000000000000</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cae3-2202">**Example value:** 00000000 — 0000 - 0000 - 0000 — 000000000000 : 00000000 — 0000 - 0000 - 0000 — 000000000000</span></span>  |  <span data-ttu-id="5cae3-2203">&bull;Non è stato possibile determinare l'identificatore del tenant.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cae3-2203">&bull; The tenant identifier could not be determined.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="5cae3-2204">Può accadere se l'endpoint ha eseguito l'accesso a una distribuzione Skype for Business Server locale.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cae3-2204">This may happen if endpoint is signed in to an on-premise Skype for Business Server deployment.</span></span>  |
| <span data-ttu-id="5cae3-2205">Building Name Pair</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cae3-2205">Building Name Pair</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="5cae3-2206">Coppia enumerata</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cae3-2206">Enumerated pair</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="5cae3-2207">Coppia del nome edificio per il primo e il secondo endpoint.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cae3-2207">Pair of the building name for the first and second endpoint.</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="5cae3-2208">&bull;Il nome dell'edificio per un endpoint non può essere determinato.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cae3-2208">&bull; The building name for an endpoint could not be determined.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="5cae3-2209">Può accadere perché l'endpoint si trova all'esterno della rete aziendale o accede alla rete da un sito senza mappatura della subnet.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cae3-2209">This could be because the endpoint is located outside the corporate network, or is accessing the network from a site without a subnet mapping.</span></span> <br/> <span data-ttu-id="5cae3-2210">**Valore di esempio:** Edificio principale: edificio del sito filiale</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cae3-2210">**Example value:** Main Building : Branch Site Building</span></span> |
| <span data-ttu-id="5cae3-2211">Inside Corp Pair</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cae3-2211">Inside Corp Pair</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="5cae3-2212">Coppia enumerata</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cae3-2212">Enumerated pair</span></span> <br/><span data-ttu-id="5cae3-2213">**Valori possibili:**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cae3-2213">**Possible values:**</span></span> <br/> <span data-ttu-id="5cae3-2214">Interno : Interno</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cae3-2214">Inside : Inside</span></span> <br/> <span data-ttu-id="5cae3-2215">Interno : Esterno</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cae3-2215">Inside : Outside</span></span> <br/> <span data-ttu-id="5cae3-2216">Esterno : Esterno</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cae3-2216">Outside : Outside</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="5cae3-2217">Coppi che mostra se gli endpoint erano situati all'interno o all'esterno della rete aziendale in base alla mappatura della subnet.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cae3-2217">Pair showing if the endpoints were located inside or outside the corporate network based on the subnet mapping.</span></span>   |   |

||||

### <a name="notes-on-dimension-data-typeunits"></a><span data-ttu-id="5cae3-2224">Note sul tipo di dati dimensione/unità</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cae3-2224">Notes on dimension data type/units</span></span>

#### <a name="boolean"></a><span data-ttu-id="5cae3-2225">Boolean</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cae3-2225">Boolean</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="5cae3-2226">I valori booleani sono sempre true o false.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cae3-2226">Boolean values are always either True or False.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="5cae3-2227">In alcuni casi, true può essere rappresentato anche come 1 e false può essere rappresentato come 0.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cae3-2227">In some cases, True can also be represented as 1 and False can be represented as 0.</span></span>

#### <a name="range"></a><span data-ttu-id="5cae3-2228">Intervallo</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cae3-2228">Range</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="5cae3-2229">Le dimensioni fornite come intervallo o gruppo di valori sono indicate utilizzando il formato seguente:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cae3-2229">Dimensions that are provided as range or group of values are shown using the following format:</span></span>

 <span data-ttu-id="5cae3-2230">_\<stringa\> ordine di ordinamento\<[limite inferiore\> - \<incluso il limite superiore esclusivo\>_</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cae3-2230">_\<sort order string\> [\<lower bound inclusive\> - \<upper bound exclusive\>_</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="5cae3-2231">Ad esempio, la dimensione Durata (Minuti) rappresenta la durata della chiamata in secondi e il valore è riferito come intervallo di valori.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cae3-2231">For example, the Duration (Minutes) dimension represents the call duration in seconds with the value reported as a range of values.</span></span>

|<span data-ttu-id="5cae3-2232">Duration (Minutes)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cae3-2232">Duration (Minutes)</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="5cae3-2233">Interpretazione</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cae3-2233">How to interpret</span></span> |
|:--- |:--- |
|<span data-ttu-id="5cae3-2234">062: [0 - 0)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cae3-2234">062: [0 - 0)</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="5cae3-2235">Durata flusso = 0 minuti</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cae3-2235">Stream duration = 0 minutes</span></span> |
|<span data-ttu-id="5cae3-2236">064: [1 - 2)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cae3-2236">064: [1 - 2)</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="5cae3-2237">1 minuto < = durata flusso < 2 minuti</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cae3-2237">1 minute < = stream duration < 2 minutes</span></span> |
|<span data-ttu-id="5cae3-2238">065: [2 - 3)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cae3-2238">065: [2 - 3)</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="5cae3-2239">2 minuti < = durata flusso < 3 minuti</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cae3-2239">2 minutes < = stream duration < 3 minutes</span></span> |
|<span data-ttu-id="5cae3-2240">066: [3 – 4)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cae3-2240">066: [3–4)</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="5cae3-2241">3 minuti < = durata flusso < 4 minuti</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cae3-2241">3 minutes < = stream duration < 4 minutes</span></span> |
|  | |

<span data-ttu-id="5cae3-2242">La \<stringa di ordinamento> viene usata per controllare l'ordinamento quando si presentano i dati e può essere usato per il filtro.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cae3-2242">The \<sort order string> is used to control the sort order when presenting the data and can be used for filtering.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="5cae3-2243">Ad esempio, un filtro su Durata (Minuti) < "065", mostrerà flussi con una durata inferiore a 2 minuti (lo "0" iniziale è necessario perché il filtro funzioni come previsto).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cae3-2243">For example, a filter on Duration (Minutes) < "065", would show streams with duration less than 2 minutes (The leading '0' is needed for the filter to work as expected).</span></span>

> [!NOTE]
> <span data-ttu-id="5cae3-2244">Il valore effettivo della stringa di ordinamento non è significativo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cae3-2244">The actual value of the sort order string isn't significant.</span></span>

#### <a name="enumeration-strings"></a><span data-ttu-id="5cae3-2245">Stringhe di enumerazione</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cae3-2245">Enumeration strings</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="5cae3-2246">Le stringhe usate da Call Quality dashboard sono spesso derivate dai file di dati e possono essere quasi tutte le combinazioni di caratteri nella lunghezza consentita.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cae3-2246">Strings used by CQD are often derived from data files, and these can be nearly any combination of character within the allowed length.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="5cae3-2247">Alcune dimensioni sembrano stringhe, ma poiché possono essere solo uno di un breve elenco di valori predefiniti, sono enumerazioni e non vere stringhe.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cae3-2247">Some dimensions look like strings, but since they can only be one of a short list of predefined values, they are enumerations and not true strings.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="5cae3-2248">Alcune stringhe di enumerazioni vengono usate anche in coppie.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cae3-2248">Some enumerations strings are also used in pairs.</span></span>

#### <a name="enumeration-pair"></a><span data-ttu-id="5cae3-2249">Coppia di enumerazione</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cae3-2249">Enumeration pair</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="5cae3-2250">Le dimensioni fornite come coppia di enumerazione sono indicate utilizzando il formato seguente:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cae3-2250">Dimensions that are provided as an enumeration pair are shown using the following format:</span></span>

 <span data-ttu-id="5cae3-2251">_\<valore di enumerazione da un punto\> finale \<: valore di enumerazione dall'altro endpoint\>_</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cae3-2251">_\<enumeration value from one end point\> : \<enumeration value from the other endpoint\>_</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="5cae3-2252">L'ordinamento dei valori di enumerazione è coerente ma non riflette l'ordinamento del primo e del secondo endpoint.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cae3-2252">The ordering of the enumeration values is consistent but doesn't reflect ordering of the first or second endpoints.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="5cae3-2253">Ad esempio, la coppia dettagli di connessione di rete mostra i valori dei dettagli di connessione di rete dei due endpoint:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cae3-2253">For example, the Network Connection Detail Pair shows the Network Connection Detail values for the two endpoints:</span></span>

|<span data-ttu-id="5cae3-2254">Network Connection Detail Pair</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cae3-2254">Network Connection Detail Pair</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="5cae3-2255">Interpretazione</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cae3-2255">How to interpret</span></span> |
|:--- |:--- |
|<span data-ttu-id="5cae3-2256">Cablata : Cablata</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cae3-2256">Wired : Wired</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="5cae3-2257">Il primo e il secondo endpoint usavano entrambi connessioni ethernet cablate.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cae3-2257">First and second endpoints both used wired ethernet connections.</span></span> |
|<span data-ttu-id="5cae3-2258">Cablata : WiFi</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cae3-2258">Wired : wifi</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="5cae3-2259">Il primo endpoint usava una connessione ethernet cablata mentre il secondo endpoint usava una connessione WiFi oppure il secondo endpoint usava una connessione ethernet cablata mentre il primo endpoint usava una connessione WiFi.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cae3-2259">First endpoint used wired ethernet connection and second endpoint used Wi-Fi connection, or the second endpoint used wired ethernet connection and first endpoint used Wi-Fi connection.</span></span> |
|<span data-ttu-id="5cae3-2260">: WiFi</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cae3-2260">: wifi</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="5cae3-2261">Il primo endpoint usava una connessione WiFi e la connessione di rete usata dal secondo endpoint era sconosciuta oppure il secondo endpoint usava una connessione WiFi e la connessione di rete usata dal primo endpoint era sconosciuta.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cae3-2261">First endpoint used a WiFi connection and the network connection used by the second endpoint is unknown, or the second endpoint used a WiFi connection and the network connection used by the first endpoint is unknown.</span></span> |
| | |

#### <a name="blank-values"></a><span data-ttu-id="5cae3-2262">Valori vuoti</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cae3-2262">Blank values</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="5cae3-2263">Nella tabella sopra riportata sono elencati i motivi possibili per cui una dimensione potrebbe essere vuota.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cae3-2263">The table above lists possible reasons why a dimension may be blank.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="5cae3-2264">Molte dimensioni e misurazioni saranno vuote se la dimensione del record QoE disponibile è falsa.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cae3-2264">Many dimensions and measurements will be blank if the QoE Record Available dimension is false.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="5cae3-2265">In genere questa situazione si verifica quando non è stato possibile effettuare la chiamata.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cae3-2265">This typically occurs when the call wasn't successfully established.</span></span>

## <a name="measurements"></a><span data-ttu-id="5cae3-2266">Misure</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cae3-2266">Measurements</span></span>

|<span data-ttu-id="5cae3-2272">Total Stream Count</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cae3-2272">Total Stream Count</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="5cae3-2273">Numero di flussi</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cae3-2273">Number of streams</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="5cae3-2274">Numero di flussi del supporto, indipendentemente dal tipo di supporto.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cae3-2274">Number media streams regardless of type of media.</span></span> |

## <a name="filters"></a><span data-ttu-id="5cae3-2786">Filtri</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cae3-2786">Filters</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="5cae3-2787">Molti valori di dimensione e misura possono essere usati anche come filtri.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cae3-2787">Many Dimension and Measurement values can also be used as filters.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="5cae3-2788">È possibile usare i filtri della query per eliminare le informazioni nello stesso modo in cui si seleziona una dimensione o una misurazione per aggiungere o includere informazioni nella query.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5cae3-2788">You can use filters in your query to eliminate information in the same way you'd select a Dimension or Measurement to add or include information in the query.</span></span>
